					Saul, HWV 53 (Handel, George Frideric)				</h1>

<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1738 (23 July to 15 August, completed 27 September)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
